It is declared outside of 'for' loop for performance reason to avoid\n  // stack allocation and unnecessary std::string's memory adjustments for each iteration. The\n  // actual value of the header is accessed via 'value' variable which is initialized differently\n  // depending whether stream_info and valid or nullptr. Based on performance tests implemented in\n  // header_formatter_speed_test.cc this approach strikes the best balance between performance and\n  // readability.\n  std::string value_buffer;\n  for (const auto& [key, entry] : headers_to_add_) {\n    absl::string_view value;\n    if (stream_info != nullptr) {\n      value_buffer = entry->formatter_->formatWithContext(context, *stream_info);\n      value = value_buffer;\n    } else {\n      value = entry->original_value_;\n    }\n    if (!value.empty() || entry->add_if_empty_) {\n      switch (entry->append_action_) {\n        PANIC_ON_PROTO_ENUM_SENTINEL_VALUES;\n      case HeaderValueOption::APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n        headers_to_add.emplace_back(key, value);\n        break;\n      case HeaderValueOption::ADD_IF_ABSENT:\n        if (auto header_entry = headers.get(key); header_entry.empty()) {\n          headers_to_add.emplace_back(key, value);\n        }\n        break;\n      case HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS:\n        if (headers.get(key).empty()) {\n          break;\n        }\n        FALLTHRU;\n      case HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n        headers_to_overwrite.emplace_back(key, value);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // First overwrite all headers which need to be overwritten.\n  for (const auto& header : headers_to_overwrite) {\n    headers.setReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);\n  }\n\n  // Now add headers which should be added.\n  for (const auto& header : headers_to_add) {\n    headers.addReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);\n  }\n}\n\nHttp::HeaderTransforms HeaderParser::getHeaderTransforms(const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& stream_info,\n                                                         bool do_formatting) const {\n  Http::HeaderTransforms transforms;\n","numLines":80,"startLine":139,"totalLines":261}}}

Investigation Report: Duplicate Response Headers in Envoy Filter Pipeline\n\n## Summary\n\nResponse headers configured via `response_headers_to_add` in route configuration are being duplicated in local replies (responses generated by the router filter itself, such as upstream timeouts or connection failures) because `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is invoked twice in the response header processing pipeline: once in the filter manager's local reply lambda and again in the router filter's `modify_headers_` callback.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause is a **double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()`** on the same response header map during local reply processing.\n\n### Technical Details\n\nWhen a local reply is generated (e.g., cluster not found, upstream timeout), the flow is:\n\n1. **Filter Manager's Local Reply Lambda** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:1123-1129` and `1156-1162`)\n   - Calls `streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders()` at line 1125/1158\n   - Then invokes the `modify_headers` callback (router's lambda)\n\n2. **Router's modify_headers_ Lambda** (`source/common/router/router.cc:444-461`)\n   - Calls `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()` at line 453\n\nThis results in the same response headers being processed twice by `finalizeResponseHeaders()`, which invokes the header parser twice.\n\n3. **Header Parser** (`source/common/router/header_parser.cc:145-213`)\n   - For headers with `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` action (default), uses `headers.addReferenceKey()` (line 211)\n   - This appends the header value\n   - When called twice, the header is appended twice, resulting in duplication\n\n## Evidence\n\n### File: `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n**sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain** (lines 1109-1145):\n```cpp\nvoid DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain(\n    bool is_grpc_request, Code code, absl::string_view body,\n    const std::function<void(ResponseHeaderMap& headers)>& modify_headers, ...) {\n  Utility::sendLocalReply(\n      state_.destroyed_,\n      Utility::EncodeFunctions{\n          [this, modify_headers](ResponseHeaderMap& headers) -> void {\n            if (streamInfo().route() && streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()) {\n              streamInfo().route()->routeEntry()->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, streamInfo());  // FIRST CALL\n            }\n            if (modify_headers) {\n              modify_headers(headers);  // Calls router's modify_headers_ which calls finalizeResponseHeaders AGAIN\n            }\n          },\n          // ... other functions\n      },\n      // ...);\n}\n```\n\n**sendDirectLocalReply** (lines 1147-1190):\n- Same issue: calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` at line 1158, then calls `modify_headers` at line 1161\n\n### File: `source/common/router/router.cc`\n\n**Router Filter's decodeHeaders** (lines 444-461):\n```cpp\nmodify_headers_ = [this](Http::ResponseHeaderMap& headers) {\n  if (route_entry_ == nullptr) {\n    return;\n  }\n  if (modify_headers_from_upstream_lb_) {\n    modify_headers_from_upstream_lb_(headers);\n  }\n  route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders(headers, callbacks_->streamInfo());  // LINE 453: SECOND CALL\n  if (attempt_count_ == 0 || !route_entry_->includeAttemptCountInResponse()) {\n    return;\n  }\n  headers.setEnvoyAttemptCount(attempt_count_);\n};\n```\n\n**Local Reply Sites** (lines 522, 550, 750, 931, etc.):\n```cpp\ncallbacks_->sendLocalReply(route_entry_->clusterNotFoundResponseCode(), \"\", modify_headers_,\n                           absl::nullopt,\n                           StreamInfo::ResponseCodeDetails::get().ClusterNotFound);\n```\n\n### File: `source/common/router/header_parser.cc`\n\n**HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders** (lines 145-213):\n```cpp\nfor (const auto& [key, entry] : headers_to_add_) {\n  // ... format the value ...\n  switch (entry->append_action_) {\n    case HeaderValueOption::APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n      headers_to_add.emplace_back(key, value);  // Default action\n      break;\n    case HeaderValueOption::OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD:\n      headers_to_overwrite.emplace_back(key, value);\n      break;\n    // ... other cases ...\n  }\n}\n// First overwrite all headers\nfor (const auto& header : headers_to_overwrite) {\n  headers.setReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);\n}\n// Then add headers\nfor (const auto& header : headers_to_add) {\n  headers.addReferenceKey(header.first, header.second);  // APPENDS the header\n}\n```\n\nWhen `finalizeResponseHeaders()` is called the first time, `addReferenceKey()` appends the header. When called the second time, `addReferenceKey()` appends it again, resulting in two copies.\n\n### File: `source/common/http/utility.cc`\n\n**Utility::prepareLocalReply** (lines 709-781):\n```cpp\nif (encode_functions.modify_headers_) {\n  encode_functions.modify_headers_(*response_headers);  // LINE 719: Invokes the filter manager's lambda\n}\n```\n\nThis invokes the filter manager's lambda that was created in `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain` or `sendDirectLocalReply`, which in turn calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` twice.\n\n### File: `api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto`\n\n**HeaderValueOption** (lines 429-481):\n```proto\nenum HeaderAppendAction {\n  APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD = 0;      // Default: appends to existing headers\n  ADD_IF_ABSENT = 1;\n  OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD = 2;   // Overwrites existing headers\n  OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS = 3;          // Only overwrites if header exists\n}\n\nmessage HeaderValueOption {\n  HeaderValue header = 1;\n  google.protobuf.BoolValue append = 2;  // Deprecated, defaults to APPEND behavior\n  HeaderAppendAction append_action = 3;   // Defaults to APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD\n  bool keep_empty_value = 4;\n}\n```\n\nThe default `append_action` is `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` (line 441), which means headers are appended by default. When `finalizeResponseHeaders()` runs twice with this action, the header is appended twice.\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`source/common/router/router.cc`** - Router filter that sets up `modify_headers_` callback with `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call\n2. **`source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`** - DownstreamFilterManager that calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its local reply lambda before invoking the router's `modify_headers_` callback\n3. **`source/common/router/header_parser.cc`** - HeaderParser that applies headers via append/overwrite operations\n4. **`source/common/http/utility.cc`** - HTTP Utility that processes the EncodeFunctions and invokes the modify_headers callback\n5. **`api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto`** - Proto definitions for HeaderValueOption with append_action field\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Response headers appear twice in HTTP responses for local replies (observed in access logs or client responses)\n   - Example: `x-custom-trace: abc123` appears twice\n   - Observed in responses where `response_code_details=upstream_response_timeout` or similar local reply details\n\n2. **Intermediate Hop 1**: Router filter sets up a `modify_headers_` callback during request decoding\n   - `router.cc:444-461` - Lambda is created that will call `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n3. **Intermediate Hop 2**: Local reply generation occurs (e.g., cluster not found)\n   - `router.cc:522` and other sites - `sendLocalReply()` is called with the `modify_headers_` callback\n\n4. **Intermediate Hop 3**: Filter manager receives the sendLocalReply call\n   - `filter_manager.cc:982-1053` - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` is invoked\n   - Determines to send the reply via the filter chain\n\n5. **Intermediate Hop 4**: Filter manager creates a response headers lambda\n   - `filter_manager.cc:1123-1129` - Creates an `EncodeFunctions` struct with a lambda that:\n     - Calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` (FIRST TIME)\n     - Calls the router's `modify_headers_` callback (which calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` SECOND TIME)\n\n6. **Intermediate Hop 5**: Utility prepares the local reply\n   - `utility.cc:719` - `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` invokes the `modify_headers_` callback\n   - This is the filter manager's lambda, which triggers the double invocation\n\n7. **Intermediate Hop 6**: Header parser processes the headers\n   - `header_parser.cc:173-212` - `evaluateHeaders()` runs and applies `response_headers_to_add`\n   - For `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, uses `addReferenceKey()` which appends\n\n8. **Root Cause**: Double header application due to `finalizeResponseHeaders()` being called twice\n   - First call: Headers are added/appended\n   - Second call: Headers are added/appended again\n   - With `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` action, results in duplicate header values\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe fix should eliminate the double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` during local reply processing. There are two potential approaches:\n\n**Option A (Recommended)**: Remove the `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from the filter manager's local reply lambda\n- Keep the call only in the router's `modify_headers_` callback\n- Modify `filter_manager.cc:1123-1129` and `1156-1162` to not call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` directly\n- This way, route-specific response headers are only finalized once, by the router filter\n\n**Option B**: Modify the router filter to not call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its `modify_headers_` callback when used for local replies\n- This would require tracking whether `modify_headers_` is being invoked for a local reply or an upstream response\n- More complex but maintains current filter manager behavior\n\n### Diagnostic Steps\n\nTo verify the issue:\n\n1. **Check Access Logs**: Look for response headers appearing twice in 5xx responses (local replies)\n   - Filter for `response_code_details=upstream_response_timeout` or similar local reply codes\n   - Compare with 200 responses to see that duplicates don't appear there\n\n2. **Count Header Occurrences**: Use a test with specific route configuration\n   ```yaml\n   response_headers_to_add:\n     - header:\n         key: \"x-test-header\"\n         value: \"test-value\"\n       append_action: OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD\n   ```\n   - For `OVERWRITE_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`, the header should appear once (double-write makes it a single header)\n   - Test scenario: Trigger cluster not found error\n   - Verify header count matches expectation\n\n3. **Enable Debug Logging**: Add logging in `HeaderParser::evaluateHeaders()` to see when it's called\n   - Confirm it's called twice for local reply cases\n\n4. **Test Upstream vs Local Replies**:\n   - Configure a route with `response_headers_to_add`\n   - Send request that gets upstream response: header appears once (expected)\n   - Send request that triggers local reply: header may appear twice (bug)\n\n### Code References for Investigation\n\n- **Router filter initialization**: `/workspace/source/common/router/router.cc:444-461` - `modify_headers_` lambda definition\n- **Router filter local reply calls**: `/workspace/source/common/router/router.cc:522, 550, 750, 931, 1002, 1058, 1338, 1405, 2235, 2254` - Various `sendLocalReply()` calls with `modify_headers_`\n- **Filter manager local reply processing**: `/workspace/source/common/http/filter_manager.cc:982-1145` - `sendLocalReply()` and `sendLocalReplyViaFilterChain()` implementations\n- **Header parser**: `/workspace/source/common/router/header_parser.cc:145-213` - `evaluateHeaders()` where headers are actually applied\n- **Proto defaults**: `/workspace/api/envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto:429-481` - `HeaderValueOption` with default `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD`\n- **Header parser initialization**: `/workspace/source/common/router/header_parser.cc:53-76` - `HeadersToAddEntry` constructor handling both deprecated `append` and newer `append_action` fields\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1990,"cache_read_input_tokens":51186,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1990},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b8aa5476-4f6a-40a7-ba2f-b35b49cbe5d7","uuid":"7f4a3c57-6ed5-4755-bc54-c74c1a9bb4a5"}

`router.cc:444-461` - Lambda is created that will call `route_entry_->finalizeResponseHeaders()`\n\n3. **Intermediate Hop 2**: Local reply generation occurs (e.g., cluster not found)\n   - `router.cc:522` and other sites - `sendLocalReply()` is called with the `modify_headers_` callback\n\n4. **Intermediate Hop 3**: Filter manager receives the sendLocalReply call\n   - `filter_manager.cc:982-1053` - `DownstreamFilterManager::sendLocalReply()` is invoked\n   - Determines to send the reply via the filter chain\n\n5. **Intermediate Hop 4**: Filter manager creates a response headers lambda\n   - `filter_manager.cc:1123-1129` - Creates an `EncodeFunctions` struct with a lambda that:\n     - Calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` (FIRST TIME)\n     - Calls the router's `modify_headers_` callback (which calls `finalizeResponseHeaders()` SECOND TIME)\n\n6. **Intermediate Hop 5**: Utility prepares the local reply\n   - `utility.cc:719` - `Utility::prepareLocalReply()` invokes the `modify_headers_` callback\n   - This is the filter manager's lambda, which triggers the double invocation\n\n7. **Intermediate Hop 6**: Header parser processes the headers\n   - First call: Headers are added/appended\n   - Second call: Headers are added/appended again\n   - With `APPEND_IF_EXISTS_OR_ADD` action, results in duplicate header values\n\n## Recommendation\n\n### Fix Strategy\n\nThe fix should eliminate the double invocation of `finalizeResponseHeaders()` during local reply processing. There are two potential approaches:\n\n**Option A (Recommended)**: Remove the `finalizeResponseHeaders()` call from the filter manager's local reply lambda\n- Keep the call only in the router's `modify_headers_` callback\n- Modify `filter_manager.cc:1123-1129` and `1156-1162` to not call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` directly\n- This way, route-specific response headers are only finalized once, by the router filter\n\n**Option B**: Modify the router filter to not call `finalizeResponseHeaders()` in its `modify_headers_` callback when used for local replies\n- This would require tracking whether `modify_headers_` is being invoked for a local reply or an upstream response\n- More complex but maintains current filter manager behavior\n\n### Diagnostic Steps\n\nTo verify the issue:\n\n1. **Check Access Logs**: Look for response headers appearing twice in 5xx responses (local replies)\n   -
